Perhaps some time later, cultivators within the marvel will be puzzled why the Demon Eye no longer blinks.

But this has nothing to do with Lu Ye anymore; his journey is considered perfectly completed, fulfilling the task assigned to him by the Dwarf Race, and next, he plans to bring the Core back to Jade Conch for placement.

This way, in a short time, Jade Conch will have a sufficiently strong backing, no longer needing to worry about any crises erupting within the Star System.

However, looking at the Core in front of him, about ten feet long and resembling a grotto-like structure, Lu Ye felt a bit at a loss.

How could he transport such a large thing back to Jade Conch?

After thinking for a while, Lu Ye activated the Small Flower World, attempting to use it to take in the Core, which would simplify matters if successful.

However, the result disappointed Lu Ye; the Small Flower World couldn't accommodate the Core of Mount Fangcun.

It's not surprising, considering the Small Flower World even has a limit on the number of cultivators it can accommodate; its scale isn't large. Though the Mount Fangcun Core doesn't appear large, it is ultimately a domain unto itself; how could the Small Flower World contain it?

Since the Small Flower World can't accommodate it, there was no point in considering the storage ring.

Can't possibly have him carry it, right? That would be ridiculous!

But Lu Ye soon realized he might be able to activate this Core like using a magic treasure.

Essentially, this was possible because of having refined the Origin of the Core.

Realizing this, Lu Ye's heart calmed; although it might look awkward, as long as he could transport the Core back to Jade Conch, it wouldn't be a problem.

Having planned his next actions, Lu Ye formed a plan.

Soon, inside the Core World, Lu Ye's voice resonated: "The domain's blockade has been broken. Those who wish to leave may do so freely."

After a moment, shadows soared towards the sky, followed quickly by others.

Moments later, all the Red Talisman Society cultivators appeared before Lu Ye. Though they had already received Lu Ye's affirming reply earlier, truly escaping the domain that had trapped them for years still couldn't help but fill their hearts with joy, giving a feeling of rebirth.



============================================================
Chapter 1809: Chapter 1809 - 1807: Homeward Journey
============================================================

The cultivators in the Core World, apart from those like Yang Ling and Hu Dequan who were specifically dispatched by the Dwarf Race, mostly ended up there by accident.

Previously, they were all honing themselves within the marvel.

Everyone has their own origins, and now that they've jumped out of the rut, they naturally won't stay.

Many cultivators expressed their gratitude to Lu Ye one by one, exchanged audio talisman markings, and said their farewells.

No matter what, they all have shared a life-and-death battle, which is not ordinary camaraderie, and given the previous circumstances, the fact they persisted in staying at the Red Talisman Society instead of defecting to Sacred Blood Summit is a testament to their character and integrity.

It can be said that if these surviving cultivators don't encounter accidents, they will have considerable achievements in the future.

Soon, the surviving cultivators of the Red Talisman Society left, seven or eight out of ten.

Lu Ye looked at the remaining Yang Ling and Hu Dequan: "What are your plans, you two?"

Yang Ling scratched his head: "No plans, not sure where to go."

After a considerable amount of time spent interacting, Lu Ye knew a bit about Yang Ling's situation. He was adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child and grew up in Mount Fangcun, so while others can each return to their homes, he indeed has nowhere to go.

"Fellow Daoist Lu, now that the Core World blockade has been broken, if the core is taken away from this marvel, without the isolation of the marvel's power, will the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge together?" Yang Ling asked.

"That's right, that's also my next plan."

The same was instructed by the Dwarf Race.

"Alright then, I'll stay inside the Core World, waiting for Mount Fangcun to merge." He came from the Southern Mount Fangcun, so to him, the Southern Region is home, and staying here he can wait to reunite with family, naturally not wanting to exert more effort.

"Old Hu, how about you? Want to return and see your homeland?" Yang Ling turned to look at Hu Dequan.

Hu Dequan pondered briefly, then shook his head, saying: "Nothing worth seeing, I'll keep you company."

Hu Dequan's situation is different from Yang Ling's; he wasn't adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child but was recruited.

The Dwarf Race has its criteria for recruiting foreign cultivators. They generally don't recruit those with strong backgrounds, as they are difficult to manage, so they recruit those with good potential but little background.

Hu Dequan's domain is just a large domain, and he has no roots in his homeland. Even if he returns, with so many years passed, things would probably be quite different.

"Hahaha." Yang Ling laughed heartily, patting his shoulder: "Then let's see who of us brothers ascends to Sun Blaze first!"

Lu Ye heard this and immediately reminded them: "You two, don't attempt to refine any of the resources within the Core World, especially the Spirit Jade Vein."

The will of the Treasure Blood Avatar has been completely obliterated, but the power of treasure blood still has residues in the Origin, and all resources within the domain have remnants of saintliness, including the Spirit Jade Vein. Xiang Yin and her sister can rely on it for cultivation because they are themselves the original Blood Race.

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan cannot, unless they want to be tainted by saintliness, which is certainly not what they desire. Having persisted for so many years, they shouldn't break their own perseverance after victory.

As they spoke, Lu Ye handed over a storage ring: "Not much, make do with it, I'll arrange things soon, then resources won't be lacking."

He brought a lot of spirit jade and spirit crystals initially, but it was only prepared for himself. When he arrived at the Core World, he gave a batch of resources to the Red Talisman Society. Later, cooperating with the Society, he distributed more, and now the resources he has left are indeed few.

However, the Talent Tree fuel is also depleted, and for now, he doesn't plan to cultivate.

Yang Ling accepted readily: "We're all brothers, no need for politeness."

Hu Dequan nudged him, muttering: "Not brothers..."

He hadn't forgotten that Lu Ye's Dao companion is Su Yuqing; in terms of seniority, Lu Ye is indeed a Master Uncle.

The two returned to the Core World.

Lu Ye looked at the ten-foot long fake mountain ahead, then leapt onto it, with his mind he moved, and the core shot forward like an arrow leaving the string.

Along the way, floating land and meteorites were shattered upon collision. Lu Ye had no intention to change direction, just maneuvering the core as a starboat, which required minimal effort.

When steering a starboat, at minimum, you must exert your own mana, whereas controlling the core requires none. After refining the Origin, Lu Ye felt the core became akin to a part of his body.

Although it was not fully refined, with some barriers still present, it caused little influence.

As for whether such collisions might harm the core... it's entirely unnecessary to worry; after all, it's a part of the stellar space supreme treasure, impossible to damage so easily.

With no concerns and an urgency to hurry, Lu Ye naturally pushed the core's speed to the utmost he could control—not the ultimate speed, but the highest level at which he could adjust directions when something needed avoidance upfront.

Not due to fear of damaging the core, but because the long road ahead, if speeding beyond control and crashing into a domain, causing devastation, the guilt would be immense.

In mere days, he passed beyond the range of the marvel's influence, having applied Origin Power to place a ban on the core in advance, so even if he took the core away from the marvel, the three parts of Mount Fangcun wouldn't instantly merge.

He plans to lift this ban once back in the Nine Provinces.

Leaving the marvel, Lu Ye immersed his mind, using the seven-color Divine Lotus to search for the channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Returning via the Soul Race ancestral land to Jade Conch was his only option; otherwise, relying solely on flying, who knows how many years it would take to traverse the distance. Moreover, Lu Ye had no idea where Jade Conch might be located.

A thorough investigation yielded no results.

This meant there were no channels nearby leading to the Soul Race ancestral land. Unperturbed, Lu Ye continued flying forward, occasionally sensing his surroundings.

The Soul Race ancestral land had many channels connecting it to the outside world; as long as he flew far enough, he was sure to sense the location of one such channel.

If all else failed, he could simply retrace his steps back to the All Phenomena Ocean.

Such a journey was incredibly tedious. Lu Ye had to constantly remain vigilant and could not afford to be distracted by cultivation. Fortunately, half a month later, when he once again immersed his mind, he finally sensed a faint connection thanks to the seven-color Divine Lotus.

As expected, that direction held a channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Lu Ye immediately adjusted the core's direction, flying toward that position.

As time passed, that connection gradually became clearer, though the distance remained vast.

Days later, seated atop the core, Lu Ye suddenly observed distant scenes, and under the enhancement of Insight Spirit Runes, a sight unfolded before his eyes that made him furrow his brow.

A domain lay ahead within the Void, but at this moment, it was under invasion by foreign enemies.

The invading force was unmistakably a giant insect hive!

The insect hive floated not far outside the domain. Although it was much smaller in scale, the battle on the Void battlefield was exceedingly fierce.

Lu Ye clearly saw numerous cultivators forming a defense line outside the domain, resisting the invading Insect Race. Around the battlefield, countless corpses and debris drifted.

This was undoubtedly a domain conflict, an invasion war.

Years ago, the four galaxies faced such invasions. Without Lu Ye bringing in the Dancing Girl, the domain might have been conquered by the Insect and Blood Races.

In the stellar space, insect hives like these seeking invasion targets were not particularly numerous, but they were not few either. Every such gigantic insect hive was equivalent to a drifting domain.

Before discovering a target to invade, the Insect Race rested and thrived. Once a target was found, they launched an all-out assault. Typically, life in the domain conquered by such insect hives was entirely wiped out. The Insect Race would remain in the domain for some years before exhausting its resources and departing, leaving the invaded domain in ruin, devoid of life.

Many dead stars in the stellar space originated in this manner.

Lu Ye neither knew which star system this was nor which domain was being invaded, but encountering such a situation, he decided not to stand idly by.

If he lacked the ability to intervene, so be it. But at this moment, he possessed the ability to intervene, and exterminate the Insect Race was undoubtedly the right action.

He immediately changed direction, piloting the core directly toward the gigantic insect hive.

Initially, neither side in the Void combat noticed anything amiss. The intensity of the battle left no room for distraction.

But as Lu Ye approached, his presence was eventually exposed.

The first to spot him was a Sun Blaze insect!

Outside the chaotic Void battlefield was a separate battleground — a Sun Blaze confrontation zone. There, two Sun Blaze insects joined forces against a human Sun Blaze, their strengths seemingly evenly matched. Faced with two opponents, the human Sun Blaze was clearly in a precarious situation.

Even so, it wasn't easy for the insect Sun Blaze to kill him.

As Lu Ye piloted the core closer to the battlefield, one of the Sun Blaze insects suddenly broke away from the fight and, with wings flapping behind it, rushed toward Lu Ye.

Before getting close, a powerful Divine Soul Power assaulted him.

Sitting atop the core, Lu Ye didn't even make a sound, but simply tilted his head and fell over.

Seeing this, the insect Sun Blaze couldn't help but snort, "Overestimating oneself!"

Though he dismissed Lu Ye as insignificant, the core beneath Lu Ye puzzled him due to its exceptional nature — it was no ordinary item — though what it truly was remained unknown.

Regardless of its nature, acquiring it seemed prudent. Thus thinking, he reached toward the core, ready to grasp it.

Already slumped on the core, Lu Ye abruptly opened his eyes, calmly staring at him, showing no signs of injury.

The insect Sun Blaze hesitated, but before he could react, a consuming force exploded, engulfing him entirely.

Next, his vision blurred, and the once raucous conflict vanished utterly, leaving him inexplicably in an unfamiliar world.

Looking around, he discovered four figures encircling him, and sensing their presence, he was greatly astonished — all four were at the Moon Jade Late Stage!



============================================================
Chapter 1807: Chapter 1807 - 1805: Becoming the Cage
============================================================

From the perspective of the Red Talisman Society, the Treasure Blood Avatar of the Blood Ancestor seemed to have appeared out of nowhere, and its emergence was incredibly bizarre and mysterious.

"The Treasure Blood Avatar of the Blood Ancestor!" Lu Ye replied.

"Treasure Blood Avatar?" A group of Red Talisman Society cultivators showed expressions of surprise and doubt.

"The Blood Clan possesses a Sacred Trait, a secret technique that involves refining their own Essence Blood to condense Treasure Blood, which, when further refined, can become a doppelganger. You should know that the split of Mount Fangcun years ago had traces of the Blood Ancestor. The Blood Ancestor left a drop of Treasure Blood here, intending to erode the core and claim it. Over the years, that drop of Treasure Blood developed its own spiritual intelligence, continuing the will of the Blood Ancestor."

Through Lu Ye's explanation, everyone finally understood the origin of that strange woman.

They also finally understood why after being bathed in the Blood Rain of this realm, cultivators possessed the Sacred Trait, as it was entirely due to the power of the Blood Ancestor's Treasure Blood.

In today's battle, Lih Tian had long planned to sacrifice himself for righteousness because only in this way could he assist the Treasure Blood Avatar in descending into the Core World.

As for the many cultivators on Sacred Blood Summit... Lih Tian did not care about their lives at all. In fact, even if they did not die at the hands of the Red Talisman Society's cultivators, with the advent of the Treasure Blood Avatar, the cultivators of Sacred Blood Summit would be slaughtered entirely.

For the Treasure Blood Avatar, all first-generation Blood Race are nourishment to strengthen itself, a primal craving she cannot resist.

Hearing all this, the group of Red Talisman Society cultivators felt both saddened and fortunate.

Through so many years of persistence and hardship, there were those among them who wavered, living within the Red Talisman Society was like being a rat, hiding everywhere and constantly facing pressure from Sacred Blood Summit while lacking cultivation resources.

People kept betraying them...

But today, they finally rejoiced in their perseverance, the conviction they held for many years finally had its reward, otherwise, where would they be alive now?

"Now, what's the situation?" Hu Dequan asked again, "Where is the Treasure Blood Avatar?"

Lu Ye looked towards the location of the Origin: "She must have gone to erode the Origin."

At those words, everyone's expressions turned heavy; although they did not understand the intricacies, everyone knew that if the Treasure Blood Avatar were to erode the Origin, this realm would undergo a drastic change.

In the countless years of resisting against Sacred Blood Summit, they barely had a foothold. But if the Origin was eroded by the Blood Ancestor's power, they would likely have no chance of survival.

Moreover, the key point was that they could not leave this place!

Previously, during the fight over the Black Abyss, as long as they held out long enough, all invading enemies would be expelled from this space, and they would naturally be able to leave.

But this time, all the people from Sacred Blood Summit were dead, and they saw no hope of leaving.

And given the current situation, they couldn't leave anyway.

"What should we do?" Yang Ling asked, although uncertain of what to do, they couldn't just wait idly.

Lu Ye shook his head; honestly, he didn't know what to do now. Previously, he used the power of the Talent Tree to ease the eroding state of the Origin, so the Talent Tree could play a role in the confrontation between the Origin and the Blood Ancestor's power.

But the key was that the Treasure Blood Avatar was too powerful; he had barely managed to save his own life under Veteran Fang's protection, and wouldn't dare to approach recklessly now.

At that moment, an anomaly suddenly occurred towards the direction of the Origin, with the Void trembling as red and white lights suddenly burst forth, illuminating the entire space.

Everyone simultaneously turned to look in that direction, and though they couldn't see precisely what was happening, just from the colors fluctuating, everyone could vaguely gauge the strengths and weaknesses of the confrontation.

The white light undoubtedly represented the power of the Origin, while the red was the Treasure Blood Avatar; this was easy to discern.

The confrontation over there suddenly entered an extremely fierce stage at that moment!

However, what made everyone anxious was that the red light clearly held an absolute advantage, and the white was significantly being eroded.

At a distance, it looked like a snow-white canvas rapidly being stained with red.

In barely one incense stick's time, there was not a hint of white left in view, only a complete red glow remaining.

Everyone's hearts sank to rock bottom!

Nevertheless, at that instant, in the midst of the intense blood-colored red glow, a dazzling white light suddenly shone through, incredibly bright.

Everyone couldn't help but feel invigorated and expectant...

The red and white intertwined incessantly, soon mixing together and becoming indistinguishable from each other.

Immediately after, the light in the distance rapidly expanded within the field of vision.

"Why is it... coming towards us?" Hu Dequan suddenly jolted, his expression turning panicky. During such a clash between powerful beings, even someone as high up as Moon Jade would only be like small fry.

"Quick, get out of the way!" Yang Ling's stern shout caused the numerous cultivators of the Red Talisman Society to quickly disperse.

Lu Ye didn't move because when the red and white light surged towards him, Veteran Fang's urgent voice sounded in his mind, "Kid, this old man has merged with her completely, considered a thorough imprisonment. The rest is up to you, open up your Divine Sea!"

In an instant, Lu Ye grasped Veteran Fang's intent.

The old man clearly knew the powerful refining force of the Talent Tree, so he placed his last hope on Lu Ye. This is likely why he exerted effort to save Lu Ye at the critical moment from his perspective; the Dao Tree lineage is the only force in the world that can truly resolve the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood, no one else can.

He had fought against the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood for countless years, always at a disadvantage with no hope of victory. Lu Ye's arrival undoubtedly gave him this opportunity.

Originally, he planned to wait until after this Black Abyss contest to carefully formulate a plan with Lu Ye. He was confident that he could use Lu Ye's power to resolve the crisis that had troubled him for countless years.

But fate was unkind; the Treasure Blood Avatar descended into the Origin space, making plans impossible in this moment of crisis; there was no choice but to risk everything, exposing his own aura while saving Lu Ye, attracting the Avatar's corrosion.

At this moment, the Origin contained not only the Origin's own power, but the treasure blood had fully integrated as well. Without external interference, it wouldn't take long before the treasure blood completely corroded the Origin, allowing the Avatar to control this realm.

Yet the Avatar was unaware that this approach also bound her, the Origin now a cage trapping her within.

If the Avatar had sufficient spiritual intelligence, she might perceive some clues, but her spiritual intelligence was ultimately naive, unable to withstand Veteran Fang's cunning.

Lu Ye opened his Divine Sea. In the next moment, he saw a sphere of light fly directly into his body.

Even though Veteran Fang controlled it with all his might, the powerful force was still beyond what Lu Ye could bear. Upon impact, he felt as though every bone shattered, dizziness overcame him, and he flew backward.

Dazed and on the brink of unconsciousness, he couldn't feel the pain in his body.

Until Veteran Fang's voice echoed beside his ears, "Wake up, don't fall asleep!"

Lu Ye bit his tongue tip, barely awake, steadied himself, and checked his own condition, confirming he wouldn't die, then quickly submerged his consciousness.

The next moment, his psyche spirit body manifested within the Divine Sea.

Raising his eyes, a red-white sphere of light came into view; it was undoubtedly the manifestation of the Origin. Initially, when Lu Ye saw it, it was surrounded by a faint blood mist, but now it had entirely transformed.

Since it was within his Divine Sea, Lu Ye could keenly sense two mighty wills engaged in a fierce struggle within the sphere.

The alternating red and white hues rocked the surroundings, waves surged from convulsing seas, even with the shimmering glow of the seven-color Divine Lotus, there were signs it might not hold.

"Hurry and refine!" Veteran Fang's voice rose like a thunderclap.

Lu Ye was about to invoke the Talent Tree's power but suddenly realized a problem: "Veteran Fang, if I refine it, what will happen to you?"

In the Origin, it's not only the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood that's trapped—if Lu Ye refines it, he can indeed eliminate the treasure blood's power, but simultaneously the Origin's consciousness would also be refined. Lu Ye can't choose to refine only the treasure blood and not the Origin; both have blended together, impossible to separate.

Veteran Fang's voice replied, "I'm pleased you asked this question, but there's no perfect solution. I became a cage at great effort, managing to trap this barghest. I won't let my work come to naught; you refine without worrying about me."

Lu Ye remained silent.

Veteran Fang knew his heart, sighing involuntarily, "You must know if the Origin is corrupted by the Blood Ancestor's power and breaks free, the entire Mount Fangcun would suffer catastrophe. Besides, as long as Mount Fangcun exists, new consciousness of the Origin will sooner or later be born."

Though the new consciousness might not be Veteran Fang.

Lu Ye's expression turned solemn, his deep tone resonated, "Veteran Fang, my apologies!"

As he finished speaking, the phantom of the Talent Tree appeared abruptly behind his psyche spirit body, an imposing towering tree with countless burning leaves.

From beneath its roots, numerous tendrils stretched out like living creatures, piercing into the Origin.

Refinement began!

A cloud of black smoke rose from the Talent Tree, a sign of the Blood Ancestor's power, harmful rather than impurities.

Seeming aware, within the Origin, the treasure blood's consciousness fiercely resisted, stirring the entire Origin into turmoil, echoing an apocalypse within Lu Ye's Divine Sea.

The seven-color Divine Lotus's radiance grew ever more brilliant, light like invisible hands calming the turmoil in Lu Ye's Divine Sea, easing his burden.

Within the Origin, Veteran Fang exerted ferocity, restraining the treasure blood.

Only then did Lu Ye have the chance to divert part of his spirit to retrieve and swallow healing elixir pills, restoring the injuries of his physical body.

Swiftly, he took out a large quantity of fire-type treasures to begin refining.

Gratefully, he had the foresight to prepare ample fire-type treasures; otherwise, with such consumption, the Talent Tree's refining might not last long.



============================================================
Chapter 1808: Chapter 1808 - 1806: Escape from Imprisonment
============================================================

In the initial period of refining, Lu Ye's Divine Sea was in turmoil, with waves surging. Although the spiritual intelligence nurtured within the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood was ignorant, it had the instinct to seek advantages and avoid harm. The refining process by the Talent Tree made it sense a crisis, causing it to struggle incessantly.

Relying solely on Lu Ye's ability, it was absolutely impossible to suppress it.

However, with the Origin Will serving as a cage, coupled with the treasure blood's prior attempt to invade the Origin, this caused it to be closely merged with the Origin. Unless it could completely suppress the Origin Will, it could not separate from the Origin.

The reaction within the Divine Sea was a direct feedback of the confrontation between the Origin Will and the treasure blood's will.

During the continuous refining, the fuel reserves of the Talent Tree were constantly being consumed. Lu Ye could feel a mysterious power transforming into nourishment for himself from the Origin.

The most noticeable change was that he could clearly perceive that his saintliness had increased rapidly and terrifyingly!

This was natural; the saintliness of the Blood Race originates from the Blood Ancestor. How terrifying is the saintliness contained in a drop of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood? Since ancient times, perhaps no creature has ever had such an opportunity, but now, by a stroke of luck, Lu Ye obtained it.

The constant and substantial increase in saintliness brought him a profound understanding of Blood Race secret techniques. Many mysteries regarding Blood Race secret techniques seemed to be inherently sealed within his body, revealed as his saintliness increased.

Previously, his saintliness was already strong enough; no Blood Race could compare with him in this world. However, he had never devoted much thought to Blood Race secret techniques, so even though his saintliness was strong, there were surely many within the Blood Race whose accomplishments in Blood Race secret techniques surpassed his.

Now it was different. Lu Ye felt that even those Blood Race Sun Blaze who had lived for countless years couldn't match his accomplishments in Blood Race secret techniques. This was a passive enhancement during the refining of treasure blood, and if he invested time to study this path in the future, the results would be even better.

Day after day of refining, the disturbances in the Divine Sea began to diminish.

Lu Ye could clearly sense that within that ball of Origin, both the will of Veteran Fang and the will of the treasure blood were continuously being worn down and weakened.

Three years passed in a flash.

In the Origin space, Lu Ye sat cross-legged, motionless.

Yang Ling was guarding by the side, as were most of the Red Talisman Society cultivators who were still alive, gathered nearby.

During these three years, they had remained here, having also searched for a way out, but to no avail. Initially, they were panicked; even during the fight against the Sacred Blood Summit, their situation was dire, but at least they had some freedom.

In this Origin space, however, they lost even that freedom, and with scarce cultivation resources, nearly everyone thought they would be trapped and die here.

Until one day, Lu Ye, taking a break from his busy efforts, sent a message to Hu Dequan, briefly explaining the situation. Only then did everyone finally feel at ease and waited here.

They waited for three years.

Until today, when Lu Ye suddenly opened his eyes, his gaze somewhat unfocused, with a sense of having been transported across time.

He hadn't expected that refining the Origin would take him so long. The root cause was a single issue—the fuel reserves of the Talent Tree were insufficient!

If he refined with all his might without regard for consequences, the efficiency would undoubtedly be faster, but the consumption of the Talent Tree's fuel would also be greater, leading to considerable unnecessary waste.

Thus, he could only control the refining efficiency to ensure the utilization rate of the Talent Tree's fuel. As a result, it took more time.

Fortunately, three years of effort bore fruit. Currently, the fuel for the Talent Tree was exhausted; though the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood within the Origin was not yet completely refined, the blood's will had been nearly obliterated, so the problem was not significant. He only needed to replenish the Talent Tree's fuel and spend a little more time refining it.

Hu Dequan, sensing something, looked over joyfully and exclaimed, "Brother Lu, you're finally awake!"

Yang Ling also quickly looked over, eagerly asking, "What's the situation now?"

Lu Ye snapped out of his daze and said, "Basically, there are no more issues."

Everyone was overjoyed, their faces filled with eager excitement.

Hu Dequan hesitated for a moment but couldn't help asking, "And the will of the Origin..."

Lu Ye remained silent for a while before saying, "I'll unlock the seal of this space first and then we'll talk after we get out."

The seal and opening of the Origin space were originally controlled by Veteran Fang. Now that he was gone, and with Lu Ye having basically refined the Origin, he naturally could control it.

Speaking as such, he concentrated his thoughts.

The Red Talisman Society cultivators, who had waited for three years, suddenly felt a change in the heavens and the earth. When they regained their senses, they found themselves already back in the Core World.

The next moment, ripples formed in the Void. Lu Ye stepped out, followed by the only remaining two Blood Servants.

"Finally back!" Yang Ling exhaled a deep breath, with a look of having narrowly escaped death. Being trapped in the Origin space for three whole years had truly been suffocating.

Hu Dequan looked at the surviving Red Talisman Society cultivators and sighed. Three years ago, before the battle began, there were over forty of them. Now, upon returning, only a dozen remained.

Fortunately, everyone from the Sacred Blood Summit, top to bottom, perished. From now on, there would be no enemies within this domain.

Soon, Hu Dequan thought of a question, "Brother Lu, can the seal of this domain also be broken now? Can we go home?"

Whether dispatched here by the Dwarf Race or inadvertently drifting into this world, they had stayed too long, always fighting against the Sacred Blood Summit. Now, having finally achieved victory, they naturally wanted to leave as soon as possible.

Lu Ye sensed slightly and nodded, "Anytime, but everyone please wait a moment, I need to prepare."

The Core World's blockade was Veteran Fang's handiwork, utilizing the power of that external marvel to isolate the Core from attracting the other three mounts of Mount Fangcun. If not for this, Mount Fangcun would have long since merged back into one entity, which would be a disaster for the Dwarf Race, for by then, the power of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood would spread throughout Mount Fangcun, and once the Blood Rain falls, all the Dwarf Race would be tainted by saintliness.

Veteran Fang's actions were to protect the Dwarf Race.

Right now, Lu Ye, having refined the Origin, controls the power of this domain and can naturally break through the domain's blockade.

"No problem, then we look forward to good news from our fellow Daoist!" Yang Ling replied cheerfully.

The members of the Red Talisman Society departed, while Xiang Yin and her sister remained, serving on the side, remembering the fallen Zhou Ran and Wang Taisheng, their hearts undeniably filled with sadness.

Although before Lu Ye arrived, the sisters would constantly spar with them, there was still a tacit understanding in the larger scheme.

When Wang Taisheng initially pledged allegiance to Lu Ye, he had only one wish, which was to leave this accursed place before he died. The reason he was willing to sincerely pledge allegiance was that compared to Lih Tian, he had greater confidence in the strongly saintly Lu Ye.

Unfortunately, this wish ultimately could not be fulfilled.

On that day of battle, if not for Lu Ye daringly activating the Small Flower World to take them in, the two sisters would not have survived.

A moment later, Lu Ye opened his eyes, revealing a contemplative look.

Xuan Yu stepped forward, "Venerable Lord, do you have any instructions?"

Lu Ye shook his head and looked towards a certain direction, "There is a Spirit Jade vein over there, you can go and cultivate."

This realm now has no enemies, so naturally they don't need to serve at his side, and even if there were enemies, given Lu Ye's current special status in this realm, even a Sun Blaze could be crushed by him with a flip of his hand.

After saying this, Lu Ye leaped into the Void, disappearing from sight.

The two sisters exchanged a glance, then flew towards the direction Lu Ye indicated, indeed finding that Spirit Jade vein.

At this moment, Lu Ye had already exited the Core World and arrived outside; the domain's blockade could seal other cultivators, but it couldn't seal him.

Surrounding him was a slightly familiar environment, presumably inside the Illusory Blood Devil's Eye Marvel.

Lu Ye suddenly thought of a question...

The name of the Illusory Blood Devil's Eye Marvel comes from the Demon Eye's blinking, and according to existing information, the Demon Eye's blinking was a manifestation of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood power, which then caused some effects on the marvel.

Now, with the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood gone, within this marvel, the Demon Eye likely won't blink anymore; although the marvel's inherent characteristics will remain, it will be somewhat misnamed.

Perhaps some time later, cultivators within the marvel will be puzzled why the Demon Eye no longer blinks.

But this has nothing to do with Lu Ye anymore; his journey is considered perfectly completed, fulfilling the task assigned to him by the Dwarf Race, and next, he plans to bring the Core back to Jade Conch for placement.

This way, in a short time, Jade Conch will have a sufficiently strong backing, no longer needing to worry about any crises erupting within the Star System.

However, looking at the Core in front of him, about ten feet long and resembling a grotto-like structure, Lu Ye felt a bit at a loss.

How could he transport such a large thing back to Jade Conch?

After thinking for a while, Lu Ye activated the Small Flower World, attempting to use it to take in the Core, which would simplify matters if successful.

However, the result disappointed Lu Ye; the Small Flower World couldn't accommodate the Core of Mount Fangcun.

It's not surprising, considering the Small Flower World even has a limit on the number of cultivators it can accommodate; its scale isn't large. Though the Mount Fangcun Core doesn't appear large, it is ultimately a domain unto itself; how could the Small Flower World contain it?

Since the Small Flower World can't accommodate it, there was no point in considering the storage ring.

Can't possibly have him carry it, right? That would be ridiculous!

But Lu Ye soon realized he might be able to activate this Core like using a magic treasure.

Essentially, this was possible because of having refined the Origin of the Core.

Realizing this, Lu Ye's heart calmed; although it might look awkward, as long as he could transport the Core back to Jade Conch, it wouldn't be a problem.

Having planned his next actions, Lu Ye formed a plan.

Soon, inside the Core World, Lu Ye's voice resonated: "The domain's blockade has been broken. Those who wish to leave may do so freely."

After a moment, shadows soared towards the sky, followed quickly by others.

Moments later, all the Red Talisman Society cultivators appeared before Lu Ye. Though they had already received Lu Ye's affirming reply earlier, truly escaping the domain that had trapped them for years still couldn't help but fill their hearts with joy, giving a feeling of rebirth.



============================================================
Chapter 1809: Chapter 1809 - 1807: Homeward Journey
============================================================

The cultivators in the Core World, apart from those like Yang Ling and Hu Dequan who were specifically dispatched by the Dwarf Race, mostly ended up there by accident.

Previously, they were all honing themselves within the marvel.

Everyone has their own origins, and now that they've jumped out of the rut, they naturally won't stay.

Many cultivators expressed their gratitude to Lu Ye one by one, exchanged audio talisman markings, and said their farewells.

No matter what, they all have shared a life-and-death battle, which is not ordinary camaraderie, and given the previous circumstances, the fact they persisted in staying at the Red Talisman Society instead of defecting to Sacred Blood Summit is a testament to their character and integrity.

It can be said that if these surviving cultivators don't encounter accidents, they will have considerable achievements in the future.

Soon, the surviving cultivators of the Red Talisman Society left, seven or eight out of ten.

Lu Ye looked at the remaining Yang Ling and Hu Dequan: "What are your plans, you two?"

Yang Ling scratched his head: "No plans, not sure where to go."

After a considerable amount of time spent interacting, Lu Ye knew a bit about Yang Ling's situation. He was adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child and grew up in Mount Fangcun, so while others can each return to their homes, he indeed has nowhere to go.

"Fellow Daoist Lu, now that the Core World blockade has been broken, if the core is taken away from this marvel, without the isolation of the marvel's power, will the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge together?" Yang Ling asked.

"That's right, that's also my next plan."

The same was instructed by the Dwarf Race.

"Alright then, I'll stay inside the Core World, waiting for Mount Fangcun to merge." He came from the Southern Mount Fangcun, so to him, the Southern Region is home, and staying here he can wait to reunite with family, naturally not wanting to exert more effort.

"Old Hu, how about you? Want to return and see your homeland?" Yang Ling turned to look at Hu Dequan.

Hu Dequan pondered briefly, then shook his head, saying: "Nothing worth seeing, I'll keep you company."

Hu Dequan's situation is different from Yang Ling's; he wasn't adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child but was recruited.

The Dwarf Race has its criteria for recruiting foreign cultivators. They generally don't recruit those with strong backgrounds, as they are difficult to manage, so they recruit those with good potential but little background.

Hu Dequan's domain is just a large domain, and he has no roots in his homeland. Even if he returns, with so many years passed, things would probably be quite different.

"Hahaha." Yang Ling laughed heartily, patting his shoulder: "Then let's see who of us brothers ascends to Sun Blaze first!"

Lu Ye heard this and immediately reminded them: "You two, don't attempt to refine any of the resources within the Core World, especially the Spirit Jade Vein."

The will of the Treasure Blood Avatar has been completely obliterated, but the power of treasure blood still has residues in the Origin, and all resources within the domain have remnants of saintliness, including the Spirit Jade Vein. Xiang Yin and her sister can rely on it for cultivation because they are themselves the original Blood Race.

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan cannot, unless they want to be tainted by saintliness, which is certainly not what they desire. Having persisted for so many years, they shouldn't break their own perseverance after victory.

As they spoke, Lu Ye handed over a storage ring: "Not much, make do with it, I'll arrange things soon, then resources won't be lacking."

He brought a lot of spirit jade and spirit crystals initially, but it was only prepared for himself. When he arrived at the Core World, he gave a batch of resources to the Red Talisman Society. Later, cooperating with the Society, he distributed more, and now the resources he has left are indeed few.

However, the Talent Tree fuel is also depleted, and for now, he doesn't plan to cultivate.

Yang Ling accepted readily: "We're all brothers, no need for politeness."

Hu Dequan nudged him, muttering: "Not brothers..."

He hadn't forgotten that Lu Ye's Dao companion is Su Yuqing; in terms of seniority, Lu Ye is indeed a Master Uncle.

The two returned to the Core World.

Lu Ye looked at the ten-foot long fake mountain ahead, then leapt onto it, with his mind he moved, and the core shot forward like an arrow leaving the string.

Along the way, floating land and meteorites were shattered upon collision. Lu Ye had no intention to change direction, just maneuvering the core as a starboat, which required minimal effort.

When steering a starboat, at minimum, you must exert your own mana, whereas controlling the core requires none. After refining the Origin, Lu Ye felt the core became akin to a part of his body.

Although it was not fully refined, with some barriers still present, it caused little influence.

As for whether such collisions might harm the core... it's entirely unnecessary to worry; after all, it's a part of the stellar space supreme treasure, impossible to damage so easily.

With no concerns and an urgency to hurry, Lu Ye naturally pushed the core's speed to the utmost he could control—not the ultimate speed, but the highest level at which he could adjust directions when something needed avoidance upfront.

Not due to fear of damaging the core, but because the long road ahead, if speeding beyond control and crashing into a domain, causing devastation, the guilt would be immense.

In mere days, he passed beyond the range of the marvel's influence, having applied Origin Power to place a ban on the core in advance, so even if he took the core away from the marvel, the three parts of Mount Fangcun wouldn't instantly merge.

He plans to lift this ban once back in the Nine Provinces.

Leaving the marvel, Lu Ye immersed his mind, using the seven-color Divine Lotus to search for the channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Returning via the Soul Race ancestral land to Jade Conch was his only option; otherwise, relying solely on flying, who knows how many years it would take to traverse the distance. Moreover, Lu Ye had no idea where Jade Conch might be located.

A thorough investigation yielded no results.

This meant there were no channels nearby leading to the Soul Race ancestral land. Unperturbed, Lu Ye continued flying forward, occasionally sensing his surroundings.

The Soul Race ancestral land had many channels connecting it to the outside world; as long as he flew far enough, he was sure to sense the location of one such channel.

If all else failed, he could simply retrace his steps back to the All Phenomena Ocean.

Such a journey was incredibly tedious. Lu Ye had to constantly remain vigilant and could not afford to be distracted by cultivation. Fortunately, half a month later, when he once again immersed his mind, he finally sensed a faint connection thanks to the seven-color Divine Lotus.

As expected, that direction held a channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Lu Ye immediately adjusted the core's direction, flying toward that position.

As time passed, that connection gradually became clearer, though the distance remained vast.

Days later, seated atop the core, Lu Ye suddenly observed distant scenes, and under the enhancement of Insight Spirit Runes, a sight unfolded before his eyes that made him furrow his brow.

A domain lay ahead within the Void, but at this moment, it was under invasion by foreign enemies.

The invading force was unmistakably a giant insect hive!

The insect hive floated not far outside the domain. Although it was much smaller in scale, the battle on the Void battlefield was exceedingly fierce.

Lu Ye clearly saw numerous cultivators forming a defense line outside the domain, resisting the invading Insect Race. Around the battlefield, countless corpses and debris drifted.

This was undoubtedly a domain conflict, an invasion war.

Years ago, the four galaxies faced such invasions. Without Lu Ye bringing in the Dancing Girl, the domain might have been conquered by the Insect and Blood Races.

In the stellar space, insect hives like these seeking invasion targets were not particularly numerous, but they were not few either. Every such gigantic insect hive was equivalent to a drifting domain.

Before discovering a target to invade, the Insect Race rested and thrived. Once a target was found, they launched an all-out assault. Typically, life in the domain conquered by such insect hives was entirely wiped out. The Insect Race would remain in the domain for some years before exhausting its resources and departing, leaving the invaded domain in ruin, devoid of life.

Many dead stars in the stellar space originated in this manner.

Lu Ye neither knew which star system this was nor which domain was being invaded, but encountering such a situation, he decided not to stand idly by.

If he lacked the ability to intervene, so be it. But at this moment, he possessed the ability to intervene, and exterminate the Insect Race was undoubtedly the right action.

He immediately changed direction, piloting the core directly toward the gigantic insect hive.

Initially, neither side in the Void combat noticed anything amiss. The intensity of the battle left no room for distraction.

But as Lu Ye approached, his presence was eventually exposed.

The first to spot him was a Sun Blaze insect!

Outside the chaotic Void battlefield was a separate battleground — a Sun Blaze confrontation zone. There, two Sun Blaze insects joined forces against a human Sun Blaze, their strengths seemingly evenly matched. Faced with two opponents, the human Sun Blaze was clearly in a precarious situation.

Even so, it wasn't easy for the insect Sun Blaze to kill him.

As Lu Ye piloted the core closer to the battlefield, one of the Sun Blaze insects suddenly broke away from the fight and, with wings flapping behind it, rushed toward Lu Ye.

Before getting close, a powerful Divine Soul Power assaulted him.

Sitting atop the core, Lu Ye didn't even make a sound, but simply tilted his head and fell over.

Seeing this, the insect Sun Blaze couldn't help but snort, "Overestimating oneself!"

Though he dismissed Lu Ye as insignificant, the core beneath Lu Ye puzzled him due to its exceptional nature — it was no ordinary item — though what it truly was remained unknown.

Regardless of its nature, acquiring it seemed prudent. Thus thinking, he reached toward the core, ready to grasp it.

Already slumped on the core, Lu Ye abruptly opened his eyes, calmly staring at him, showing no signs of injury.

The insect Sun Blaze hesitated, but before he could react, a consuming force exploded, engulfing him entirely.

Next, his vision blurred, and the once raucous conflict vanished utterly, leaving him inexplicably in an unfamiliar world.

Looking around, he discovered four figures encircling him, and sensing their presence, he was greatly astonished — all four were at the Moon Jade Late Stage!



============================================================
Chapter 1808: Chapter 1808 - 1806: Escape from Imprisonment
============================================================

In the initial period of refining, Lu Ye's Divine Sea was in turmoil, with waves surging. Although the spiritual intelligence nurtured within the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood was ignorant, it had the instinct to seek advantages and avoid harm. The refining process by the Talent Tree made it sense a crisis, causing it to struggle incessantly.

Relying solely on Lu Ye's ability, it was absolutely impossible to suppress it.

However, with the Origin Will serving as a cage, coupled with the treasure blood's prior attempt to invade the Origin, this caused it to be closely merged with the Origin. Unless it could completely suppress the Origin Will, it could not separate from the Origin.

The reaction within the Divine Sea was a direct feedback of the confrontation between the Origin Will and the treasure blood's will.

During the continuous refining, the fuel reserves of the Talent Tree were constantly being consumed. Lu Ye could feel a mysterious power transforming into nourishment for himself from the Origin.

The most noticeable change was that he could clearly perceive that his saintliness had increased rapidly and terrifyingly!

This was natural; the saintliness of the Blood Race originates from the Blood Ancestor. How terrifying is the saintliness contained in a drop of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood? Since ancient times, perhaps no creature has ever had such an opportunity, but now, by a stroke of luck, Lu Ye obtained it.

The constant and substantial increase in saintliness brought him a profound understanding of Blood Race secret techniques. Many mysteries regarding Blood Race secret techniques seemed to be inherently sealed within his body, revealed as his saintliness increased.

Previously, his saintliness was already strong enough; no Blood Race could compare with him in this world. However, he had never devoted much thought to Blood Race secret techniques, so even though his saintliness was strong, there were surely many within the Blood Race whose accomplishments in Blood Race secret techniques surpassed his.

Now it was different. Lu Ye felt that even those Blood Race Sun Blaze who had lived for countless years couldn't match his accomplishments in Blood Race secret techniques. This was a passive enhancement during the refining of treasure blood, and if he invested time to study this path in the future, the results would be even better.

Day after day of refining, the disturbances in the Divine Sea began to diminish.

Lu Ye could clearly sense that within that ball of Origin, both the will of Veteran Fang and the will of the treasure blood were continuously being worn down and weakened.

Three years passed in a flash.

In the Origin space, Lu Ye sat cross-legged, motionless.

Yang Ling was guarding by the side, as were most of the Red Talisman Society cultivators who were still alive, gathered nearby.

During these three years, they had remained here, having also searched for a way out, but to no avail. Initially, they were panicked; even during the fight against the Sacred Blood Summit, their situation was dire, but at least they had some freedom.

In this Origin space, however, they lost even that freedom, and with scarce cultivation resources, nearly everyone thought they would be trapped and die here.

Until one day, Lu Ye, taking a break from his busy efforts, sent a message to Hu Dequan, briefly explaining the situation. Only then did everyone finally feel at ease and waited here.

They waited for three years.

Until today, when Lu Ye suddenly opened his eyes, his gaze somewhat unfocused, with a sense of having been transported across time.

He hadn't expected that refining the Origin would take him so long. The root cause was a single issue—the fuel reserves of the Talent Tree were insufficient!

If he refined with all his might without regard for consequences, the efficiency would undoubtedly be faster, but the consumption of the Talent Tree's fuel would also be greater, leading to considerable unnecessary waste.

Thus, he could only control the refining efficiency to ensure the utilization rate of the Talent Tree's fuel. As a result, it took more time.

Fortunately, three years of effort bore fruit. Currently, the fuel for the Talent Tree was exhausted; though the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood within the Origin was not yet completely refined, the blood's will had been nearly obliterated, so the problem was not significant. He only needed to replenish the Talent Tree's fuel and spend a little more time refining it.

Hu Dequan, sensing something, looked over joyfully and exclaimed, "Brother Lu, you're finally awake!"

Yang Ling also quickly looked over, eagerly asking, "What's the situation now?"

Lu Ye snapped out of his daze and said, "Basically, there are no more issues."

Everyone was overjoyed, their faces filled with eager excitement.

Hu Dequan hesitated for a moment but couldn't help asking, "And the will of the Origin..."

Lu Ye remained silent for a while before saying, "I'll unlock the seal of this space first and then we'll talk after we get out."

The seal and opening of the Origin space were originally controlled by Veteran Fang. Now that he was gone, and with Lu Ye having basically refined the Origin, he naturally could control it.

Speaking as such, he concentrated his thoughts.

The Red Talisman Society cultivators, who had waited for three years, suddenly felt a change in the heavens and the earth. When they regained their senses, they found themselves already back in the Core World.

The next moment, ripples formed in the Void. Lu Ye stepped out, followed by the only remaining two Blood Servants.

"Finally back!" Yang Ling exhaled a deep breath, with a look of having narrowly escaped death. Being trapped in the Origin space for three whole years had truly been suffocating.

Hu Dequan looked at the surviving Red Talisman Society cultivators and sighed. Three years ago, before the battle began, there were over forty of them. Now, upon returning, only a dozen remained.

Fortunately, everyone from the Sacred Blood Summit, top to bottom, perished. From now on, there would be no enemies within this domain.

Soon, Hu Dequan thought of a question, "Brother Lu, can the seal of this domain also be broken now? Can we go home?"

Whether dispatched here by the Dwarf Race or inadvertently drifting into this world, they had stayed too long, always fighting against the Sacred Blood Summit. Now, having finally achieved victory, they naturally wanted to leave as soon as possible.

Lu Ye sensed slightly and nodded, "Anytime, but everyone please wait a moment, I need to prepare."

The Core World's blockade was Veteran Fang's handiwork, utilizing the power of that external marvel to isolate the Core from attracting the other three mounts of Mount Fangcun. If not for this, Mount Fangcun would have long since merged back into one entity, which would be a disaster for the Dwarf Race, for by then, the power of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood would spread throughout Mount Fangcun, and once the Blood Rain falls, all the Dwarf Race would be tainted by saintliness.

Veteran Fang's actions were to protect the Dwarf Race.

Right now, Lu Ye, having refined the Origin, controls the power of this domain and can naturally break through the domain's blockade.

"No problem, then we look forward to good news from our fellow Daoist!" Yang Ling replied cheerfully.

The members of the Red Talisman Society departed, while Xiang Yin and her sister remained, serving on the side, remembering the fallen Zhou Ran and Wang Taisheng, their hearts undeniably filled with sadness.

Although before Lu Ye arrived, the sisters would constantly spar with them, there was still a tacit understanding in the larger scheme.

When Wang Taisheng initially pledged allegiance to Lu Ye, he had only one wish, which was to leave this accursed place before he died. The reason he was willing to sincerely pledge allegiance was that compared to Lih Tian, he had greater confidence in the strongly saintly Lu Ye.

Unfortunately, this wish ultimately could not be fulfilled.

On that day of battle, if not for Lu Ye daringly activating the Small Flower World to take them in, the two sisters would not have survived.

A moment later, Lu Ye opened his eyes, revealing a contemplative look.

Xuan Yu stepped forward, "Venerable Lord, do you have any instructions?"

Lu Ye shook his head and looked towards a certain direction, "There is a Spirit Jade vein over there, you can go and cultivate."

This realm now has no enemies, so naturally they don't need to serve at his side, and even if there were enemies, given Lu Ye's current special status in this realm, even a Sun Blaze could be crushed by him with a flip of his hand.

After saying this, Lu Ye leaped into the Void, disappearing from sight.

The two sisters exchanged a glance, then flew towards the direction Lu Ye indicated, indeed finding that Spirit Jade vein.

At this moment, Lu Ye had already exited the Core World and arrived outside; the domain's blockade could seal other cultivators, but it couldn't seal him.

Surrounding him was a slightly familiar environment, presumably inside the Illusory Blood Devil's Eye Marvel.

Lu Ye suddenly thought of a question...

The name of the Illusory Blood Devil's Eye Marvel comes from the Demon Eye's blinking, and according to existing information, the Demon Eye's blinking was a manifestation of the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood power, which then caused some effects on the marvel.

Now, with the Blood Ancestor's treasure blood gone, within this marvel, the Demon Eye likely won't blink anymore; although the marvel's inherent characteristics will remain, it will be somewhat misnamed.

Perhaps some time later, cultivators within the marvel will be puzzled why the Demon Eye no longer blinks.

But this has nothing to do with Lu Ye anymore; his journey is considered perfectly completed, fulfilling the task assigned to him by the Dwarf Race, and next, he plans to bring the Core back to Jade Conch for placement.

This way, in a short time, Jade Conch will have a sufficiently strong backing, no longer needing to worry about any crises erupting within the Star System.

However, looking at the Core in front of him, about ten feet long and resembling a grotto-like structure, Lu Ye felt a bit at a loss.

How could he transport such a large thing back to Jade Conch?

After thinking for a while, Lu Ye activated the Small Flower World, attempting to use it to take in the Core, which would simplify matters if successful.

However, the result disappointed Lu Ye; the Small Flower World couldn't accommodate the Core of Mount Fangcun.

It's not surprising, considering the Small Flower World even has a limit on the number of cultivators it can accommodate; its scale isn't large. Though the Mount Fangcun Core doesn't appear large, it is ultimately a domain unto itself; how could the Small Flower World contain it?

Since the Small Flower World can't accommodate it, there was no point in considering the storage ring.

Can't possibly have him carry it, right? That would be ridiculous!

But Lu Ye soon realized he might be able to activate this Core like using a magic treasure.

Essentially, this was possible because of having refined the Origin of the Core.

Realizing this, Lu Ye's heart calmed; although it might look awkward, as long as he could transport the Core back to Jade Conch, it wouldn't be a problem.

Having planned his next actions, Lu Ye formed a plan.

Soon, inside the Core World, Lu Ye's voice resonated: "The domain's blockade has been broken. Those who wish to leave may do so freely."

After a moment, shadows soared towards the sky, followed quickly by others.

Moments later, all the Red Talisman Society cultivators appeared before Lu Ye. Though they had already received Lu Ye's affirming reply earlier, truly escaping the domain that had trapped them for years still couldn't help but fill their hearts with joy, giving a feeling of rebirth.



============================================================
Chapter 1809: Chapter 1809 - 1807: Homeward Journey
============================================================

The cultivators in the Core World, apart from those like Yang Ling and Hu Dequan who were specifically dispatched by the Dwarf Race, mostly ended up there by accident.

Previously, they were all honing themselves within the marvel.

Everyone has their own origins, and now that they've jumped out of the rut, they naturally won't stay.

Many cultivators expressed their gratitude to Lu Ye one by one, exchanged audio talisman markings, and said their farewells.

No matter what, they all have shared a life-and-death battle, which is not ordinary camaraderie, and given the previous circumstances, the fact they persisted in staying at the Red Talisman Society instead of defecting to Sacred Blood Summit is a testament to their character and integrity.

It can be said that if these surviving cultivators don't encounter accidents, they will have considerable achievements in the future.

Soon, the surviving cultivators of the Red Talisman Society left, seven or eight out of ten.

Lu Ye looked at the remaining Yang Ling and Hu Dequan: "What are your plans, you two?"

Yang Ling scratched his head: "No plans, not sure where to go."

After a considerable amount of time spent interacting, Lu Ye knew a bit about Yang Ling's situation. He was adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child and grew up in Mount Fangcun, so while others can each return to their homes, he indeed has nowhere to go.

"Fellow Daoist Lu, now that the Core World blockade has been broken, if the core is taken away from this marvel, without the isolation of the marvel's power, will the three parts of Mount Fangcun merge together?" Yang Ling asked.

"That's right, that's also my next plan."

The same was instructed by the Dwarf Race.

"Alright then, I'll stay inside the Core World, waiting for Mount Fangcun to merge." He came from the Southern Mount Fangcun, so to him, the Southern Region is home, and staying here he can wait to reunite with family, naturally not wanting to exert more effort.

"Old Hu, how about you? Want to return and see your homeland?" Yang Ling turned to look at Hu Dequan.

Hu Dequan pondered briefly, then shook his head, saying: "Nothing worth seeing, I'll keep you company."

Hu Dequan's situation is different from Yang Ling's; he wasn't adopted by the Dwarf Race as a child but was recruited.

The Dwarf Race has its criteria for recruiting foreign cultivators. They generally don't recruit those with strong backgrounds, as they are difficult to manage, so they recruit those with good potential but little background.

Hu Dequan's domain is just a large domain, and he has no roots in his homeland. Even if he returns, with so many years passed, things would probably be quite different.

"Hahaha." Yang Ling laughed heartily, patting his shoulder: "Then let's see who of us brothers ascends to Sun Blaze first!"

Lu Ye heard this and immediately reminded them: "You two, don't attempt to refine any of the resources within the Core World, especially the Spirit Jade Vein."

The will of the Treasure Blood Avatar has been completely obliterated, but the power of treasure blood still has residues in the Origin, and all resources within the domain have remnants of saintliness, including the Spirit Jade Vein. Xiang Yin and her sister can rely on it for cultivation because they are themselves the original Blood Race.

Yang Ling and Hu Dequan cannot, unless they want to be tainted by saintliness, which is certainly not what they desire. Having persisted for so many years, they shouldn't break their own perseverance after victory.

As they spoke, Lu Ye handed over a storage ring: "Not much, make do with it, I'll arrange things soon, then resources won't be lacking."

He brought a lot of spirit jade and spirit crystals initially, but it was only prepared for himself. When he arrived at the Core World, he gave a batch of resources to the Red Talisman Society. Later, cooperating with the Society, he distributed more, and now the resources he has left are indeed few.

However, the Talent Tree fuel is also depleted, and for now, he doesn't plan to cultivate.

Yang Ling accepted readily: "We're all brothers, no need for politeness."

Hu Dequan nudged him, muttering: "Not brothers..."

He hadn't forgotten that Lu Ye's Dao companion is Su Yuqing; in terms of seniority, Lu Ye is indeed a Master Uncle.

The two returned to the Core World.

Lu Ye looked at the ten-foot long fake mountain ahead, then leapt onto it, with his mind he moved, and the core shot forward like an arrow leaving the string.

Along the way, floating land and meteorites were shattered upon collision. Lu Ye had no intention to change direction, just maneuvering the core as a starboat, which required minimal effort.

When steering a starboat, at minimum, you must exert your own mana, whereas controlling the core requires none. After refining the Origin, Lu Ye felt the core became akin to a part of his body.

Although it was not fully refined, with some barriers still present, it caused little influence.

As for whether such collisions might harm the core... it's entirely unnecessary to worry; after all, it's a part of the stellar space supreme treasure, impossible to damage so easily.

With no concerns and an urgency to hurry, Lu Ye naturally pushed the core's speed to the utmost he could control—not the ultimate speed, but the highest level at which he could adjust directions when something needed avoidance upfront.

Not due to fear of damaging the core, but because the long road ahead, if speeding beyond control and crashing into a domain, causing devastation, the guilt would be immense.

In mere days, he passed beyond the range of the marvel's influence, having applied Origin Power to place a ban on the core in advance, so even if he took the core away from the marvel, the three parts of Mount Fangcun wouldn't instantly merge.

He plans to lift this ban once back in the Nine Provinces.

Leaving the marvel, Lu Ye immersed his mind, using the seven-color Divine Lotus to search for the channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Returning via the Soul Race ancestral land to Jade Conch was his only option; otherwise, relying solely on flying, who knows how many years it would take to traverse the distance. Moreover, Lu Ye had no idea where Jade Conch might be located.

A thorough investigation yielded no results.

This meant there were no channels nearby leading to the Soul Race ancestral land. Unperturbed, Lu Ye continued flying forward, occasionally sensing his surroundings.

The Soul Race ancestral land had many channels connecting it to the outside world; as long as he flew far enough, he was sure to sense the location of one such channel.

If all else failed, he could simply retrace his steps back to the All Phenomena Ocean.

Such a journey was incredibly tedious. Lu Ye had to constantly remain vigilant and could not afford to be distracted by cultivation. Fortunately, half a month later, when he once again immersed his mind, he finally sensed a faint connection thanks to the seven-color Divine Lotus.

As expected, that direction held a channel leading to the Soul Race ancestral land.

Lu Ye immediately adjusted the core's direction, flying toward that position.

As time passed, that connection gradually became clearer, though the distance remained vast.

Days later, seated atop the core, Lu Ye suddenly observed distant scenes, and under the enhancement of Insight Spirit Runes, a sight unfolded before his eyes that made him furrow his brow.

A domain lay ahead within the Void, but at this moment, it was under invasion by foreign enemies.

The invading force was unmistakably a giant insect hive!

The insect hive floated not far outside the domain. Although it was much smaller in scale, the battle on the Void battlefield was exceedingly fierce.

Lu Ye clearly saw numerous cultivators forming a defense line outside the domain, resisting the invading Insect Race. Around the battlefield, countless corpses and debris drifted.

This was undoubtedly a domain conflict, an invasion war.

Years ago, the four galaxies faced such invasions. Without Lu Ye bringing in the Dancing Girl, the domain might have been conquered by the Insect and Blood Races.

In the stellar space, insect hives like these seeking invasion targets were not particularly numerous, but they were not few either. Every such gigantic insect hive was equivalent to a drifting domain.

Before discovering a target to invade, the Insect Race rested and thrived. Once a target was found, they launched an all-out assault. Typically, life in the domain conquered by such insect hives was entirely wiped out. The Insect Race would remain in the domain for some years before exhausting its resources and departing, leaving the invaded domain in ruin, devoid of life.

Many dead stars in the stellar space originated in this manner.

Lu Ye neither knew which star system this was nor which domain was being invaded, but encountering such a situation, he decided not to stand idly by.

If he lacked the ability to intervene, so be it. But at this moment, he possessed the ability to intervene, and exterminate the Insect Race was undoubtedly the right action.

He immediately changed direction, piloting the core directly toward the gigantic insect hive.

Initially, neither side in the Void combat noticed anything amiss. The intensity of the battle left no room for distraction.

But as Lu Ye approached, his presence was eventually exposed.

The first to spot him was a Sun Blaze insect!

Outside the chaotic Void battlefield was a separate battleground — a Sun Blaze confrontation zone. There, two Sun Blaze insects joined forces against a human Sun Blaze, their strengths seemingly evenly matched. Faced with two opponents, the human Sun Blaze was clearly in a precarious situation.

Even so, it wasn't easy for the insect Sun Blaze to kill him.

As Lu Ye piloted the core closer to the battlefield, one of the Sun Blaze insects suddenly broke away from the fight and, with wings flapping behind it, rushed toward Lu Ye.

Before getting close, a powerful Divine Soul Power assaulted him.

Sitting atop the core, Lu Ye didn't even make a sound, but simply tilted his head and fell over.

Seeing this, the insect Sun Blaze couldn't help but snort, "Overestimating oneself!"

Though he dismissed Lu Ye as insignificant, the core beneath Lu Ye puzzled him due to its exceptional nature — it was no ordinary item — though what it truly was remained unknown.

Regardless of its nature, acquiring it seemed prudent. Thus thinking, he reached toward the core, ready to grasp it.

Already slumped on the core, Lu Ye abruptly opened his eyes, calmly staring at him, showing no signs of injury.

The insect Sun Blaze hesitated, but before he could react, a consuming force exploded, engulfing him entirely.

Next, his vision blurred, and the once raucous conflict vanished utterly, leaving him inexplicably in an unfamiliar world.

Looking around, he discovered four figures encircling him, and sensing their presence, he was greatly astonished — all four were at the Moon Jade Late Stage!

Lu Ye clearly saw numerous cultivators forming a defense line outside the domain, resisting the invading Insect Race. Around the battlefield, countless corpses and debris drifted.

This was undoubtedly a domain conflict, an invasion war.

Years ago, the four galaxies faced such invasions. Without Lu Ye bringing in the Dancing Girl, the domain might have been conquered by the Insect and Blood Races.

In the stellar space, insect hives like these seeking invasion targets were not particularly numerous, but they were not few either. Every such gigantic insect hive was equivalent to a drifting domain.

Before discovering a target to invade, the Insect Race rested and thrived. Once a target was found, they launched an all-out assault. Typically, life in the domain conquered by such insect hives was entirely wiped out. The Insect Race would remain in the domain for some years before exhausting its resources and departing, leaving the invaded domain in ruin, devoid of life.

Many dead stars in the stellar space originated in this manner.

Lu Ye neither knew which star system this was nor which domain was being invaded, but encountering such a situation, he decided not to stand idly by.

If he lacked the ability to intervene, so be it. But at this moment, he possessed the ability to intervene, and exterminate the Insect Race was undoubtedly the right action.

He immediately changed direction, piloting the core directly toward the gigantic insect hive.

Initially, neither side in the Void combat noticed anything amiss. The intensity of the battle left no room for distraction.

But as Lu Ye approached, his presence was eventually exposed.

The first to spot him was a Sun Blaze insect!

Outside the chaotic Void battlefield was a separate battleground — a Sun Blaze confrontation zone. There, two Sun Blaze insects joined forces against a human Sun Blaze, their strengths seemingly evenly matched. Faced with two opponents, the human Sun Blaze was clearly in a precarious situation.

Even so, it wasn't easy for the insect Sun Blaze to kill him.

As Lu Ye piloted the core closer to the battlefield, one of the Sun Blaze insects suddenly broke away from the fight and, with wings flapping behind it, rushed toward Lu Ye.

Before getting close, a powerful Divine Soul Power assaulted him.

Sitting atop the core, Lu Ye didn't even make a sound, but simply tilted his head and fell over.

Seeing this, the insect Sun Blaze couldn't help but snort, "Overestimating oneself!"

Though he dismissed Lu Ye as insignificant, the core beneath Lu Ye puzzled him due to its exceptional nature — it was no ordinary item — though what it truly was remained unknown.

Regardless of its nature, acquiring it seemed prudent. Thus thinking, he reached toward the core, ready to grasp it.

Already slumped on the core, Lu Ye abruptly opened his eyes, calmly staring at him, showing no signs of injury.

The insect Sun Blaze hesitated, but before he could react, a consuming force exploded, engulfing him entirely.

Next, his vision blurred, and the once raucous conflict vanished utterly, leaving him inexplicably in an unfamiliar world.

Looking around, he discovered four figures encircling him, and sensing their presence, he was greatly astonished — all four were at the Moon Jade Late Stage!
